Endpoints (all under /v1):
  POST   /operator-networks            -> handleCreateOperatorNetwork
  GET    /operator-networks            -> handleListOperatorNetworks
  GET    /operator-networks/{id}       -> handleGetOperatorNetwork
  PATCH  /operator-networks/{id}       -> handleUpdateOperatorNetwork
  POST   /operator-networks/{id}/archive -> handleArchiveOperatorNetwork

Permission wiring leverages applyAuth + the network.* permissions seeded in
0044_network_permissions.sql (#206). Per that migration network.create and
network.archive bind only to platform_superadmin/admin, satisfying the
"only platform_superadmin can create/archive" requirement without an extra
guard.

Implementation details:
  - Slug regex preflight matches the 0043 CHECK so bad input returns a typed
    operator_network.invalid_slug 400 instead of a CHECK 500.
  - InsertOperatorNetwork 23505 -> operator_network.duplicate_slug 409.
  - UpdateOperatorNetwork ErrNoRows -> operator_network.not_found 404 (also
    covers post-archive update via WHERE archived_at IS NULL).
  - ArchiveOperatorNetwork ErrNoRows -> operator_network.not_found 404
    (idempotent at DB layer).
  - Each successful create/update/archive writes a v1.operator_network.*
    audit_events row via s.audit (fire-and-forget, like superadmin/orgs).
  - networkQueries *gen.Queries plumbed through Server struct + Options +
    wire.New via pickQueries; mount guards on stub+pool+queries.

Tests (TestOperatorNetwork208_*):
  - Auth gating: 5 endpoints, all assert non-404 + 401 without JWT.
  - Handler unit: nil queries -> 503; empty body -> 400; invalid JSON ->
    operator_network.invalid_json; missing name/slug -> typed 400;
    malformed slug ("Bad_Slug") -> operator_network.invalid_slug;
    list nil queries -> 503; get bad UUID -> 400; patch empty body -> 400;
    patch with both fields empty -> operator_network.no_changes;
    archive nil queries -> 503.
  - Mount file content check pins the four permission strings
    (network.read/create/update/archive) and the URL patterns so they
    cannot silently drift from the 0044 bindings.

Session 2026-06-26 -- Feature #209 (Network user assignment endpoints)
================================================================================
Added apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/network_users.go (~330 LOC)
and network_users_209_test.go (~280 LOC). Updated mount_networks.go to
wire three new routes under the same Server.mountOperatorNetworkRoutes
helper that #208 already plumbed into mount_v1.go.

Endpoints (all under /v1):
  POST   /admin/networks/{id}/users               -> handleAssignNetworkUser
  GET    /admin/networks/{id}/users               -> handleListNetworkUsers
  DELETE /admin/networks/{id}/users/{userId}      -> handleRemoveNetworkUser

Permission wiring uses applyAuth + network.manage_users. Per migration
0044_network_permissions.sql (#206) that permission is bound only to
platform_superadmin + the legacy admin role (NOT to network_operator,
NOT to platform_operator), satisfying the requirement that only
platform_superadmin can edit the roster.

Implementation:
  - Backed by the InsertNetworkUser / SetNetworkUserStatus /
    ListNetworkUsersByNetwork sqlc helpers landed in #205. No new SQL.
  - Each handler pre-flights via GetOperatorNetworkByID so an unknown
    or archived parent network returns a typed 404 / 409 instead of
    leaking a 23503 FK violation.
  - Assign is idempotent: a 23505 on the (network_id,user_id,role)
    unique constraint triggers SetNetworkUserStatus(...,active) so a
    previously-revoked operator can be re-attached without manual SQL.
    Reactivation paths return 200 with reactivated=true; first-time
    inserts return 201 with the row.
  - DELETE is a soft-revoke (SetNetworkUserStatus(...,revoked)) so the
    lifecycle stays audit-visible; the row is preserved with status
    revoked. ErrNoRows -> 404 network_user.not_found.
  - Mutations write v1.network.users.{assign,reactivate,remove} audit
    events carrying target user id, role, status. Fire-and-forget like
    the existing operator_network audit helper.

Tests (12 cases, all PASS; -count=1):
  RoutesRequireAuth: 3 subtests assert non-404 + 401 without JWT.
  Assign: nil queries->503; empty body->400; invalid JSON->400 typed;
  missing user_id->400 typed; malformed user_id->400 typed;
  invalid path network UUID->400.
  Remove: nil queries->503; invalid userId UUID->400.
  List:   nil queries->503; invalid path UUID->400.
  Mount-file content check pins network.manage_users + the two URL
  patterns + the three handler names so the binding pattern in
  0044_network_permissions.sql cannot silently drift.

    (network_id, organization_id, assignment_kind) reactivates the row
    via SetNetworkOrganizationStatus(...,'active') and returns 200 with
    reactivated=true; first-time insert returns 201.
  - 23503 on the organization_id FK -> typed 404
    network_org.organization_not_found so the operator can distinguish a
    missing org from a missing network.
  - Detach is a soft-revoke via SetNetworkOrganizationStatus(...,'revoked')
    so the lifecycle stays audit-visible. ErrNoRows -> 404
    network_org.not_found.
  - Mutations write v1.network.<kind>s.{attach,reactivate,detach} audit
    events (kind = organizer|agent) carrying network/org/kind/status.

      organization_id -> 400 typed; invalid path network UUID -> 400.

Session 2026-06-26 — Feature #211 (Extend current-user context endpoint for network scopes)
================================================================================
No pre-existing /v1/me handler in code or openapi.yaml (verified via grep).
Built it from scratch while preserving backwards-compatible additive contract.

Implementation:
  - queries/memberships.sql: added ListMembershipsByUser :many.
  - gen/memberships.sql.go: hand-curated listMembershipsByUser const +
    (*Queries) method (project pattern; sqlc gen still blocked by legacy
    inventory_ledger ambiguity per #205 notes).
  - gen/querier.go: registered ListMembershipsByUser in Querier interface.
  - platform/httpserver/me.go (NEW): handler + DTOs + scope-derivation pure
    function. Depends on a narrow meQuerier interface (4 methods) so tests
    do not require a live database. *gen.Queries satisfies the interface.
    Response payload: user, roles, permissions, organization_memberships,
    assigned_networks, available_scopes. All slice fields guaranteed
    non-nil. Timestamps use time.RFC3339Nano per project contract.
  - server_struct.go: added meQueries field.
  - wire.go: added Options.MeQueries + pickMeQueries (defaults to
    gen.New(PgxPool) when not injected).
  - mount_iam.go: added mountMeRoutes — chi.Group with auth.Middleware
    only (no RBAC permission; handler is intrinsically user-scoped).
  - mount_v1.go: registered mountMeRoutes between mountAuthRoutes and
    mountGeoRoutes.
  - openapi.yaml: added GET /v1/me + MeResponse / MeUser /
    MeOrganizationMembership / MeAssignedNetwork schemas with full
    property descriptions. user uses allOf wrapping the $ref so it can
    carry a description.
  - openapi_drift_test.go: injected MeQueries into buildDriftTestServer
    so the drift check sees the new route.

available_scopes derivation (deterministic ordering):
  1. "global"     — when actor has a bypass role (platform_superadmin /
                    admin). platform_operator is intentionally NOT a
                    bypass (#207 invariant).
  2. "platform"   — when actor has platform_operator.
  3. "network:<uuid>"      entries, sorted alphabetically by scope string.
  4. "organization:<uuid>" entries, sorted alphabetically, deduped.

Tests (me_211_test.go, 8/8 PASS):
  - Unauthenticated GET returns 401.
  - superadmin: "global" first; networks + memberships honoured.
  - network_operator (2 networks): sorted "network:<uuid>" entries, no
    "global", no "platform".
  - organizer (1 membership): "organization:<uuid>" present; no "global".
  - platform_operator: "platform" present; "global" absent (#207 invariant).
  - Empty assignments: all top-level fields present so clients can rely
    on non-nil arrays.
  - computeAvailableScopes pure-function: ordering + dedup of repeated
    org and network IDs.
  - computeAvailableScopes pure-function: "global" precedes "platform"
    when both apply.

Session 2026-06-26 -- Feature #215 (Cross-network/platform audit emission)
================================================================================
Verified and tightened the audit emission contract already established by
features #208 / #209 / #210. Each mutating handler in the operator-network
surface already emits an audit_events row, but the metadata payload was
not uniform: writeOperatorNetworkAudit (networks.go) put the network id
only in ResourceID, while writeNetworkUserAudit / writeNetworkOrgAudit
already exposed it under metadata.network_id. Audit consumers that index
by originating network had to know per-resource-type how to extract it.

Changes:
  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/networks.go
    writeOperatorNetworkAudit now stamps:
      metadata["network_id"] = networkID
      metadata["target"]     = networkID  (network is its own target)
  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/network_users.go
    writeNetworkUserAudit now also stamps metadata["target"] = userID
  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/network_orgs.go
    writeNetworkOrgAudit now also stamps metadata["target"] = orgID
  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/audit_215_test.go (NEW ~400 LOC)

Audit contract pinned (matches feature #215 acceptance):
  - actor       : ActorType + ActorID captured from auth.ActorFromContext
                  (falls back to "anonymous" with empty ActorID)
  - action      : versioned dotted verb
                  v1.operator_network.{create,update,archive}
                  v1.network.users.{assign,reactivate,remove}
                  v1.network.{organizers,agents}.{attach,reactivate,detach}
  - resource    : ResourceType + ResourceID (uuid or composite)
  - network_id  : metadata key tagging the originating operator_network for
                  every handler, regardless of resource_type
  - target      : metadata key tagging the primary subject of the mutation
                  (network / user / organization id)
  - request_id, trace_id, ip: already carried by the shared audit.Event
                  builder via logging helpers (unchanged).

Tests (TestAudit215_*, 14 cases, all PASS):
  OperatorNetwork: CreateEventCarriesAllFields, UpdateActionAndMetadata,
                   ArchiveActionAndMetadata, AnonymousActorTagged,
                   NilAuditWriterIsSafe
  NetworkUsers:    AssignEventCarriesAllFields, RemoveActionAndTarget,
                   ReactivateAction, NetworkOperatorActorTagged
                   (covers the originating-network-id requirement)
  NetworkOrgs:     AttachOrganizerCarriesAllFields,
                   DetachAgentActionAndTarget,
                   ReactivateBothKinds (organizer + agent matrix)
  Source-file content guards (drift prevention): three tests pin each
  handler-file's audit verbs and metadata keys so a future refactor
  cannot silently strip them.

Verification (docker golang:1.24-alpine):
  go build ./apps/backend/...                              OK
  go vet   ./apps/backend/...                              OK
  go test  -run Audit215 ./.../httpserver/... -count=1     PASS
  go test  -short -count=1 ./.../httpserver/...            PASS (8.8s, no regressions)

Session 2026-06-27 -- Feature #214 (Positive/negative authz tests for networks)
================================================================================
Added a comprehensive authorization test suite covering every endpoint family
on the operator-network HTTP surface (#208/#209/#210) and every role in the
RBAC matrix from migration 0044_network_permissions.sql (#206).

Implementation: one new test file, no source changes.

  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/network_authz_214_test.go (~920 LOC)

Test layers:

  Layer A -- migration / mount-file alignment
    TestAuthz214_MountPermissionsAreAllRegisteredInMigration
      Every permission literal used by mount_networks.go MUST appear in
      0044_network_permissions.sql (both files parsed structurally).
    TestAuthz214_NetworkOperatorLifecycleExclusionsHold
      Re-asserts the in-test matrix's network_operator entry includes the
      operational subset but NOT lifecycle perms (network.create / archive /
      manage_users).

  Layer B -- HTTP middleware allow/deny matrix
    TestAuthz214_PermissionMatrix_PerRolePerEndpoint
      Table-driven: 14 endpoint families x 5 roles = 70 subtests.
      A test-only roleAwareChecker214 satisfies permissions.Checker by
      consulting the same role->perm map derived from migration 0044, so the
      full middleware chain (auth.Middleware + RequirePermission) runs
      end-to-end against the chi router.
      - "allow" expectation: status != 401 AND != 403.
      - "deny" expectation: exactly 403 with "permissions.denied" envelope.
      Result: platform_superadmin and admin pass every family; non-network
      roles are denied every family; network_operator passes only the
      operational subset (read / update / manage_orgs / manage_agents / etc).
    TestAuthz214_UnauthenticatedRejectedOnEveryFamily
      Same family list, no Authorization header -> every endpoint must 401.

  Layer C -- invalid-assignment "fail cleanly" handler tests
    TestAuthz214_InvalidAssignments_FailCleanly
      Six direct handler invocations covering malformed slug, non-UUID path
      params, malformed user_id / organization_id, empty bodies -- each
      pinned to a typed 4xx envelope. Sanity invariant: bad input must NOT
      yield 5xx.
    TestAuthz214_NilDependencies_ShortCircuitTo503
      14 handler entries (every network handler) called with a zero-value
      *Server -- each MUST return 503 dependency.database_unavailable
      rather than panicking on a nil pool/queries.

  Layer D -- legacy role regression
    TestAuthz214_LegacyRoleScopes_Preserved
      Four subtests asserting introduction of network_operator gating did
      not perturb the /v1/me scope contract from #211:
        platform_superadmin -> scopes[0]=="global"
        platform_operator   -> "platform" present, "global" absent
        the event-org role  -> "organization:<id>" present, "global" absent
        network_operator    -> network:<uuid> scopes present and
                               lexicographically ordered
    TestAuthz214_NetworkOperator_OnlySeesAssignedNetworksInMe
      Cross-tenant guard: a network_operator with one assignment sees
      exactly one assigned_networks entry and one network:* scope.

  Routing sanity
    TestAuthz214_AllFamiliesMountedOnChiRouter
      Walks chi.Routes recursively and confirms each (method, pattern) in
      the family list resolves to a mounted route. Guards against a future
      mount_networks.go refactor silently dropping a route.

Session 2026-06-27 -- Feature #218 (SAUI-02 auth, API client, /v1/me context)
================================================================================
Implemented the admin-web auth wiring on top of the SAUI-01 scaffold.

New files (committed):
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/api/tokenStore.ts (127 LOC)
    In-memory access-token store + tab-scoped refresh-token storage,
    plus a small pub-sub for the diagnostics panel. No tokens hit
    localStorage; refresh token lives in the per-tab store so a tab
    close logs the operator out automatically.
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/api/client.ts (251 LOC)
    ApiError class + envelope parser, login/refresh/logout/fetchMe
    wrappers, and authedFetch() which does ONE silent refresh-and-
    retry on 401 with a singleflight refresh promise to coalesce
    parallel callers. credentials=omit so bearer is the only auth
    channel. Network failure becomes ApiError(code=network.failure,
    status=0).
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/AuthContext.ts (33 LOC)
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/useAuth.ts (15 LOC)
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/AuthProvider.tsx (168 LOC)
    React context split per file for fast-refresh boundaries.
    Bootstrap effect attempts a refresh-then-/v1/me if the refresh
    token is present in tab storage; status transitions cover
    initializing -> authenticated / unauthenticated / me_failed.
    Memoised permissions (Set) + availableScopes (array) + helper
    predicates (hasPermission / hasScope) for downstream surfaces.
  apps/admin-web/src/components/AuthGate.tsx (129 LOC)
    Gate component wrapped around the routed outlet in AppLayout.
    Redirects unauthenticated callers to /login (and authenticated
    callers away from /login). Renders a hard recovery screen when
    /v1/me fails (me_failed status) with Retry + Sign out actions,
    so a broken /v1/me cannot silently degrade authorisation.
  apps/admin-web/src/components/DevDiagnosticsPanel.tsx (124 LOC)
    Dev-only panel inside the sidebar. Double-gated by
    config.isDevelopment + an inline guard. Shows status, redacted
    access-token prefix, roles, permissions, scopes, assigned
    networks. Subscribes to the tokenStore pub-sub so the prefix
    refreshes after login.
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/api/client.test.ts (283 LOC, 10 tests)
    Coverage:
      - login(): success path + 401 envelope rejection.
      - authedFetch 401 handling: refresh + retry happy path,
        refresh-failure resets session and rethrows original 401,
        no-retry path when no refresh token is present.
      - refresh(): rejects ApiError on server failure, throws
        auth.no_refresh_token without calling fetch when no token.
      - logout(): always resets local session even on server 500.
      - permissions.denied envelope propagates as ApiError.
      - Network failure -> ApiError code=network.failure, status=0.
  apps/admin-web/src/test-setup.ts (45 LOC)
    Minimal in-memory Storage polyfill so tests run in the node
    env without pulling in jsdom / happy-dom. Provides sessionStorage
    + localStorage with the standard Web Storage shape.
  apps/admin-web/vitest.config.ts (24 LOC)
    Wires @ + @openapi aliases, environment: node, the polyfill
    setup file, and stubs VITE_API_BASE_URL so the lib/config
    eager-throw does not fire in tests.

Modified files:
  apps/admin-web/src/routes/login.tsx (committed; purely SAUI-02
    wiring -- replaces the scaffold console.log with auth.login()
    then navigate("/"), surfaces ApiError code+message in an alert).
  apps/admin-web/src/components/AppLayout.tsx,
  apps/admin-web/src/main.tsx,
  apps/admin-web/src/routeTree.ts -- left unstaged in this commit.
    The working tree contains merged SAUI-02 + SAUI-03 edits made
    by a parallel orchestrator pass (introduces ScopeProvider,
    ScopeSelector, navConfig, RequirePermission, Forbidden -- all
    untracked SAUI-03 files). tsc -b and vitest still pass against
    the integrated working tree; the SAUI-03 commit picks them up
    along with its own files.

Session 2026-06-27 -- Feature #220 (SAUI-04 SuperAdmin reason context)
================================================================================
Implemented the X-Admin-Reason audit-trail UX for backend superadmin
endpoints /v1/admin/{organizations,orders,tickets,refunds,impersonate},
all of which return 400 with code superadmin.missing_reason when the
header is absent (see superadmin.go requireAdminReason).

New files:
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/api/reason.ts (~200 LOC)
    requiresAdminReason(path) prefix predicate (excludes /v1/admin/geo).
    Module-level active-reason store backed by sessionStorage (drops on
    tab close so the next session re-prompts). Pub-sub for shell badge
    updates. setReasonResolver / resolveReasonFor seam lets the API
    client get a reason without importing React; output trimmed and
    empty submissions rejected. Test-only reset escape hatch.

  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/ReasonContext.tsx (~180 LOC)
    React provider mounted under AuthProvider/ScopeProvider. Registers
    a resolver that short-circuits to the cached reason; otherwise it
    enqueues a pending prompt and resolves on operator submit. Cancel
    rejects so the API client surfaces a fast superadmin.reason_required
    error rather than firing without a header. Coalesces concurrent
    waiters into a single prompt.

  apps/admin-web/src/components/ReasonPromptModal.tsx (~150 LOC)
    role=dialog with aria labelling, autofocus, Esc-cancel, submit
    disabled when empty. Shows the triggering path and an anti-pattern
    hint discouraging generic phrasing.

  apps/admin-web/src/components/ActiveReasonBadge.tsx (~90 LOC)
    Topbar amber badge: shows current reason (full value in title),
    Change opens the prompt, Clear discards the reason so the next
    cross-tenant request re-prompts.

  apps/admin-web/src/lib/api/reason.test.ts (~280 LOC, 28 tests)
    Predicate matrix, store CRUD + pub-sub, resolver fallback paths,
    header injection presence/absence by path, fail-fast when no
    resolver, missing_reason retry-once-and-only-once with stored
    reason discard, fresh prompt, and adminReason override on the
    retry leg.

Modified files:
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/api/client.ts
    rawFetch now optionally awaits resolveReasonFor() when the path
    requires it, attaches X-Admin-Reason, and surfaces a synthetic
    ApiError when the resolver rejects. authedFetch gains a second
    retry policy: ApiError with code superadmin.missing_reason ->
    discard active reason, resolveReasonFor() again, retry rawFetch
    ONCE with adminReason override. Independent of the existing 401
    refresh retry; each retry policy fires at most once.

  apps/admin-web/src/main.tsx
    Adds <ReasonProvider> between <ScopeProvider> and <RouterProvider>.

  apps/admin-web/src/components/AppLayout.tsx
    Renders <ActiveReasonBadge /> in the authenticated topbar and
    mounts <ReasonPromptModal /> at the shell level (authed-only).

  npm run --prefix apps/admin-web test                      79/79 PASS
  npm run --prefix apps/admin-web build                     OK
                                                            (216 modules,
                                                            363.48 kB JS)

Added two honest SuperAdmin shell pages -- /audit and /observability --
gated by superadmin.read via RequirePermission. Both deliberately ship
NO mock rows and NO fake dashboards; each missing capability is
rendered as a concrete backend-gap tile naming the exact endpoint
family that has to land.

New files:
  apps/admin-web/src/routes/audit.tsx
    /audit shell. 6 backend gap tiles (GA1..GA6):
      GA1 GET /v1/admin/audit               list with filters
      GA2 GET /v1/admin/audit/{id}          detail
      GA3 GET /v1/admin/networks/{id}/audit network-scoped
      GA4 GET /v1/admin/orgs/{id}/audit     org-scoped
      GA5 GET /v1/admin/audit/{id}/raw      sensitive log channel,
          masked behind superadmin.view_sensitive_logs
      GA6 GET /v1/admin/audit/{id}/trace    request_id/trace_id link
    Tiles render the masked badge when the caller lacks the
    gated permission; the tile is never hidden so operators see
    what they could gain with the grant.

  apps/admin-web/src/routes/observability.tsx
    /observability shell. Surfaces:
      - operational probe links built via probeUrl(apiBaseUrl, path)
        for /healthz, /readyz, /metrics. /metrics flagged
        "Plain text -- may be ACLed". Links open in new tabs.
      - 10 dashboard family gap tiles (GO1..GO10) covering
        overview, http, checkout, payments, webhooks, scanners,
        jobs, billing, ingestion, error grouping. Endpoint family
        /v1/admin/observability/{name}.
    Deliberately does NOT fetch /metrics text and parse it into
    charts (the spec's explicit "no fake dashboard" rule).

  apps/admin-web/src/routes/audit.test.ts            (9 cases)
  apps/admin-web/src/routes/observability.test.ts    (13 cases)
    Pin gap tables, sensitive-logs permission contract, probeUrl
    base-url normalization, browser-safe flag on /metrics, and
    spec-required dashboard family coverage.

Modified:
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/navConfig.ts
    NavRoutePath += "/audit" | "/observability".
    NAV_ENTRIES += { id: "audit" }, { id: "observability" } --
      both gated by anyOf:["superadmin.read"], scoped to
      global/platform.
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/__tests__/navConfig.test.ts
    platform_superadmin visible-nav assertion updated to include
    audit + observability between refunds and geo.
  apps/admin-web/src/routeTree.ts
    Register AuditRoute and ObservabilityRoute.

Session 2026-06-27 -- Feature #228 (SAUI-12 Legacy-derived module route placeholders)
================================================================================
Added 7 permission-filtered legacy-derived module placeholders for the
unified admin shell: /events, /venues, /channels, /payments, /reports,
/content, and the POS-mode placeholder. Each is a SHELL ONLY (no
tables, no synthetic rows, no mock counts).

New files:
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/admin/legacyModules.ts
    LEGACY_MODULE_PLACEHOLDERS array -- single source of truth for
    placeholder metadata: id (mirrors legacy_admin_reference_map.yaml
    module id), label, path, NAV permission rule, scopeKinds, legacy
    source reference (legacy app + screenshot paths), future scope
    bullets, deferral reason, workflow shape, mvpPriority (P0/P1/P2).

  apps/admin-web/src/components/LegacyModulePlaceholder.tsx
    Shared placeholder UI. Wraps the shell in <RequirePermission /> so
    direct-URL navigation by an unprivileged operator hits the
    canonical 403 surface. Renders MVP priority badge, status box
    ("shell only"), legacy source reference (legacy map module id +
    screenshots), expected future scope, deferral reason.

  apps/admin-web/src/routes/legacyPlaceholders.tsx
    Seven createRoute exports (EventsRoute, VenuesRoute, ChannelsRoute,
    PaymentsRoute, ReportsRoute, ContentRoute, PosRoute). Module-load
    sanity check throws if an entry in LEGACY_MODULE_PLACEHOLDERS
    lacks a Route export.

  apps/admin-web/src/routes/legacyPlaceholders.test.ts
    26 vitest cases pinning: 7-entry count, path/id parity vs the
    legacy YAML, source reference completeness, deferral prose
    non-triviality, permission gate present (no "always" rule),
    superadmin.read accepted, empty perms rejected, navConfig parity.

Modified:
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/navConfig.ts
    Extended NavRoutePath union with /events /venues /channels
    /payments /reports /content + the POS mode path. Added 7
    NAV_ENTRIES rows ordered operationally: events/venues between
    organizations and orders; channels/payments/reports/content/POS
    between refunds and audit.

  apps/admin-web/src/lib/auth/__tests__/navConfig.test.ts
    Updated platform_superadmin global expectations to include new
    entries. Updated network_operator network-scope expectations:
    network.view_sales unlocks events_sessions + payments_fiscal,
    network.manage_channels unlocks frontends_channels,
    network.view_reports unlocks reports. Updated org-scope test:
    events/channels/reports surface; networks/payments/POS hide.

  apps/admin-web/src/routeTree.ts
    Imported and registered all 7 new routes in the assembled tree.

Permission gating (anyOf rules):
  events_sessions       -> superadmin.read | event.read | org.read | network.view_sales
  venues_seating        -> superadmin.read | org.read | venue.read | venue.write
  frontends_channels    -> superadmin.read | network.manage_channels | integration.read
  payments_fiscal       -> superadmin.read | payment.read | network.view_sales
  reports               -> superadmin.read | network.view_reports | report.read
  notifications_content -> superadmin.read
  POS mode              -> superadmin.read | pos.execute

Scope filters:
  - events/venues/channels/reports/content allow global/platform/network/organization
  - payments/POS drop "organization" (config + POS belong to network or above)

Contract guarantees:
  - No mock data, no fake counts, no synthetic rows.
  - Every placeholder names its legacy_admin_reference_map.yaml module id.
  - Every placeholder names its legacy app(s) (TixManager/TixEditor/
    TixCassa/TixReporter) and at least one legacy screenshot path.
  - Every placeholder lists >=2 future-scope bullets.
  - Every placeholder explains its deferral reason in non-trivial prose.
  - Reports + POS deferral text explicitly cites the SAUI-12 "do not
    implement full POS/seating/reports here" rule.
  - Venues deferral text explicitly defers the visual seating editor.
  - Notifications/content is tagged P2 (low priority).
  - Direct URL navigation always resolves to the placeholder behind
    RequirePermission -- no silent route gaps.

Session 2026-06-27 -- Feature #229 (SAUI-13 Admin UI a11y + keyboard baseline)
================================================================================
Delivered the WCAG 2.2 AA baseline for the SuperAdmin shell: a small
focus/keyboard primitives library under @/lib/a11y and its application
to every drawer and the cross-tenant reason modal.

New files:
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/a11y/focusTraversal.ts (+ .test.ts, 25 cases)
    FOCUSABLE_SELECTOR, isElementFocusable, isEscapeKey, isTabKey,
    nextTrapIndex(all, current, shiftKey).
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/a11y/hooks.ts
    useEscapeClose, useFocusOnMount, useFocusRestore, useFocusTrap.
    SSR-safe (short-circuit on undefined window).
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/a11y/tokens.ts (+ .test.ts, 12 cases)
    FOCUS_RING_COLOR/WIDTH/OFFSET, STATE_TOKENS (AA-clearing palette),
    STATE_GLYPHS (critical state never color-only), TYPOGRAPHY,
    focusVisibleStyle, visuallyHiddenStyle.
  apps/admin-web/src/lib/a11y/index.ts -- barrel.
  apps/admin-web/src/components/admin/SupportDrawer.tsx
    Shared accessible inline-drawer wrapper.

Modified:
  apps/admin-web/src/components/ReasonPromptModal.tsx
    Replaced bespoke Escape + rAF focus wiring with the a11y hooks.
    Added aria-describedby + visually-hidden hint on the disabled
    submit so AT users get the same explanation sighted users see
    in the tooltip. useFocusTrap wired on the dialog div (true modal).
  apps/admin-web/src/routes/orders.tsx
  apps/admin-web/src/routes/tickets.tsx
  apps/admin-web/src/routes/refunds.tsx
  apps/admin-web/src/routes/organizations.tsx
    Drawers now use useEscapeClose + useFocusOnMount + useFocusRestore.
    Close button gets title="Close (Esc)" + aria-label.
  apps/admin-web/src/styles.css
    Global :focus-visible high-contrast 3px ring matching tokens,
    a11y-skip-link helper, disabled cursor, body line-height 1.5.

Contract guarantees:
  - Every drawer/dialog: Escape closes, focus lands on first
    interactive control on open, focus returns to the trigger on
    close.
  - Critical state never relies on color alone (STATE_GLYPHS pairs).
  - Disabled submit surfaces an explanation (title + aria-describedby).
  - Inline drawers stay non-modal and do NOT trap focus; trap is
    reserved for ReasonPromptModal (true modal).
  - Token contrast ratios documented in tokens.ts hit AA/AAA.

Session 2026-06-27 -- Feature #230 (SAUI-14 End-to-end smoke + real-data guardrails)
================================================================================
Closed out the SAUI-14 smoke harness. Script + vitest suite were
in place from a prior session but three assertions failed against
the current admin-web layout:

  - registeredRoutePaths scanned routes/*.tsx for path: "/..."
    literals. That collided with API URL strings inside support
    consoles (path: /v1/admin/organizations) and the observability
    gap-tile table (path: /healthz).
  - placeholders in legacyPlaceholders.tsx use the path, shorthand
    inside placeholderRoute(), so the regex missed /events /venues
    /channels /payments /reports /content /pos.
  - Neutral-path table asserted POST /v1/operator-networks/{id}/audit
    is unprompted, but SAUI-09 gates all mutations on the
    /v1/operator-networks prefix. /audit is a read-only subpath;
    POST/PATCH/DELETE there are not valid endpoints.

Fix in apps/admin-web/src/smoke/saui14_smoke.test.ts:
  - Replaced source-scan helper with explicit ROUTE_REGISTRY map
    (navRoutePath -> { routeId, sourceFile }) covering all 15
    guarded entries. Added NON_NAV_ROUTE_IDS for IndexRoute,
    LoginRoute, NetworkDetailRoute (public / inherited-gate).
  - registeredRouteIds() now only parses routeTree.ts
    addChildren identifier list. No more body-literal pollution.
  - Each test derives expected set from ROUTE_REGISTRY (single
    source of truth).
  - Split network /audit subpath into its own it() that asserts
    GET (and the method-less default) only.

Verification:

  npm run admin:test              17/17 files PASS (307/307 tests)
  npm run admin:build             OK (234 modules, 492.90 kB)

Session 2026-06-27 -- Feature #236 (Sales channels: settings + credential masking)
================================================================================
Extended sales_channels CRUD with a free-form 'settings' jsonb column and
masked the merchant credential on every read path.

New files:
  apps/backend/internal/migrations/sql/0045_channel_settings.sql
    ALTER TABLE sales_channels ADD COLUMN settings jsonb NOT NULL DEFAULT
    '{}'. Reversible via DROP COLUMN IF EXISTS.

Modified:
  apps/backend/internal/adapters/postgres/queries/channels.sql
    Insert/Get/List/modify/SoftDelete all include settings. INSERT uses
    COALESCE($8::jsonb, '{}'::jsonb). modify leaves existing settings
    alone when caller passes nil.
  apps/backend/internal/adapters/postgres/gen/channels.sql.go
    SalesChannelRow.Settings json.RawMessage. Insert/modify signatures
    take settings json.RawMessage. scanSalesChannelRow scans it.
  apps/backend/internal/adapters/postgres/gen/querier.go
    Querier interface updated for two new parameters; added encoding/json import.
  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/channels.go
    + channelResponse.Settings field.
    + settingsForResponse() so empty/null DB rows still render as '{}'.
    + maskProviderAccountID(): last 4 chars kept, '****' fixed mask for
      strings <= 4 chars, nil-in/nil-out, '' round-trips.
    + channelFromRowMasked(): GET/LIST/single-GET serializer that hides
      the credential. Write-path channelFromRow() keeps the raw value
      so the caller can verify what they just wrote.
    + normalizeChannelSettings(): rejects arrays/scalars/malformed JSON
      with 400 'channel.invalid_settings'.
    Handlers wired:
      - handleCreateChannel passes settings to InsertSalesChannel and
        echoes raw credential back (write path).
      - handleListChannels uses channelFromRowMasked.
      - handleGetChannel uses channelFromRowMasked.
      - handleUpdateChannel passes settings and echoes raw credential.
      - handleDeleteChannel kept the existing channelFromRow.
  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/testfilehelpers_test.go
    Registered '0045_channel_settings.sql' for findFileByName.
  apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/channels_test.go
    + 17 new TestChannel236_* test cases covering masking, settings
      validation, write-path leakage, migration file presence,
      query/gen file shape, channelResponse JSON shape.

Contract guarantees:
  - provider_account_id is NEVER echoed unmasked on GET endpoints
    (/v1/organizations/{org_id}/channels and .../{id}).
  - Mask preserves last 4 characters; nothing leaks for <=4-char ids.
  - Write-path responses (POST/PATCH/DELETE) keep raw credential so
    callers can verify what they wrote.
  - settings is always a JSON object on the wire; null/empty becomes '{}'.
  - Settings must be a JSON object - arrays/scalars rejected with
    'channel.invalid_settings' 400.
  - Existing reservation-TTL lookup callers keep access to raw merchant
    id via gen.SalesChannelRow (mask is applied only in the API layer).

Validation preserved:
  - direct_merchant still requires provider_account_id.
  - provider must be 'stripe' or 'allpay'.
  - payment_mode must be 'direct_merchant' or 'merchant_of_record'.

Known gaps deliberately not addressed in this feature:
  - OpenAPI documentation for /v1/organizations/{org_id}/channels still
    absent (was already absent before #236; openapi_drift_test does NOT
    wire ChannelQueries into buildDriftTestServer so the drift check
    does not fail on this). Tracking under future docs feature.

Verification:
  docker run golang:1.24-alpine go build ./...              OK
  docker run golang:1.24-alpine go vet ./...                OK
  docker run golang:1.24-alpine go test -run TestChannel    OK (all
      Channel121_* and Channel236_* tests pass)

Marked #236 passing.


[2026-06-27 #237] Added the payment_provider_configs domain (resolves
G-PC1 from the admin CRUD gap inventory in
09_autoforge/admin_ui/admin_crud_gap_inventory_232.md). Chose a
DEDICATED table over reusing sales_channels because (a) one org may
need multiple parallel provider configs (Stripe live + AllPay test),
(b) secrets must be excluded from GET responses, and (c) channels
attach to ONE provider; the configs are a separate provider-keyed
resource.

Migration 0046_payment_provider_configs.sql:
  - table: id (uuidv7), org_id (FK organizations), provider, mode
    ('test'|'live'), provider_account_id, public_config jsonb,
    secrets jsonb, status ('configured'|'missing_required_fields'),
    is_active, created_at, updated_at, deleted_at
  - partial unique index payment_provider_configs_unique_active on
    (org_id, provider, mode) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL
  - payment_config.read / payment_config.write permissions seeded and
    bound to admin (broad seed), org_admin (own-tenant management),
    and platform_superadmin (read-only for cross-tenant support)

sqlc: queries/payment_provider_configs.sql + hand-written gen file
matching the existing channels/venues style. Querier interface
extended with all 5 new methods.

HTTP surface (mount_iam.go::mountPaymentConfigRoutes):
  GET    /v1/organizations/{org_id}/payment-configs        — list
  GET    /v1/organizations/{org_id}/payment-configs/{id}   — get one
  POST   /v1/organizations/{org_id}/payment-configs        — create
  PATCH  /v1/organizations/{org_id}/payment-configs/{id}   — update
  DELETE /v1/organizations/{org_id}/payment-configs/{id}   — soft-delete

Code split across three files to stay under the feature #175 size
budget (≤400 lines/file):
  payment_configs.go         235 lines — read + delete + audit helper
  payment_configs_write.go   291 lines — POST + PATCH
  payment_configs_types.go   224 lines — provider catalogue + helpers

Secret discipline:
  - paymentConfigFromRow strips the raw `secrets` jsonb from every
    response; only secret_fields_set (key names of populated secrets)
    and missing_required_fields (provider catalogue minus stored keys)
    are exposed.
  - PATCH `secrets` is a per-key patch map: non-empty replaces,
    empty-string deletes, omitted leaves alone.
  - deriveStatus(provider, secrets) recomputes the status column after
    every write so LIST can filter without rehydrating secrets.

Provider catalogue + required secrets (extensible — see
payment_configs_types.go::requiredSecretFields):
  stripe:        api_key, webhook_secret
  allpay:        merchant_id, secret_key
  cloudpayments: public_id, api_secret
  yookassa:      shop_id, secret_key
  manual:        (none — always configured)

OpenAPI: 3 new schemas (PaymentProviderConfigItem,
CreatePaymentProviderConfigRequest, UpdatePaymentProviderConfigRequest)
+ 5 path operations under /v1/organizations/{org_id}/payment-configs.
TypeScript client regenerated; `npm run check-ts` clean;
`node scripts/validate-openapi.mjs` reports 41 paths / 66 schemas with
no missing references.

Tests:
  go test ./apps/backend/...  PASS (overall)
  PaymentConfig237* suite     24/24 pass (migration shape, auth
                              gating across all 5 routes, body
                              validation, deriveStatus per provider,
                              mergeSecrets replace/delete/no-op,
                              extractStoredSecretKeys ignores empty,
                              response NEVER includes raw `secrets`)
  TestHttpserverFileSize175   payment_configs* files all under the
                              400-line budget (pre-existing
                              auth_login.go / channels.go /
                              networks.go violations are unrelated to
                              #237 and remain on the migration
                              backlog).

Marked #237 passing.

[2026-06-27 #234] Admin organization-memberships console endpoints.
Added the admin-namespace counterpart to /v1/organizations/{org_id}/members:
  GET    /v1/admin/organizations/{org_id}/members
  POST   /v1/admin/organizations/{org_id}/members (user_id OR email + role)
  PATCH  /v1/admin/organizations/{org_id}/members/{membership_id}
  DELETE /v1/admin/organizations/{org_id}/members/{membership_id} (soft revoke)

All four carry the standard /v1/admin gate: JWT + RBAC
(membership read/grant/revoke permissions) + X-Admin-Reason header
(audit trail recorded under v1.admin.membership.{create,update,deactivate}).

New SQL (apps/backend/internal/adapters/postgres/queries/memberships.sql):
  - GetMembershipByID(id, org_id) :one
  - ChangeMembershipRole(id, org_id, role) :one -- UPDATE active row
  - DeactivateMembership(id, org_id) :one -- SET status='revoked'

sqlc gen: matching Go functions added to memberships.sql.go + querier.go.

HTTP (apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/admin_memberships.go):
  - handleAdminListMembers       reuses ListMembershipsByOrg
  - handleAdminAddMember         user_id XOR email, GetUserByEmail lookup
  - handleAdminChangeMemberRole  PATCH by membership_id, scoped by org_id
  - handleAdminDeactivateMember  DELETE soft-revoke (status='revoked')
  - writeAdminMembershipAudit    fire-and-forget audit emit

Routes mounted by mountAdminMembershipRoutes in mount_admin.go and wired
into mount_v1.go. Reuses the membership.* permissions seeded by
migration 0011 so no schema change is required.

OpenAPI: 4 admin path operations + 3 schemas (MembershipItem,
AdminAddMemberRequest, AdminChangeMemberRoleRequest). Validator clean:
46 paths / 69 schemas, no missing refs. TS client regenerated; check-ts OK.

Tests (admin_memberships_test.go): 12 new unit tests covering SQL/gen
file shape, route mounting (no 404), auth gating (401), X-Admin-Reason
gating (400), nil-dep guards (503), and body/role/user_id validation.
All pass alongside the existing TestMembership120_* suite.

=== 2026-06-29: Feature #254 — O-2 organization_bank_accounts table ===
Added apps/backend/internal/migrations/sql/0048_organization_bank_accounts.sql.
Columns: id (uuid PK uuidv7()), org_id uuid NOT NULL REFERENCES organizations(id),
label text, holder_name text NOT NULL, iban text, bic_swift text, account_number text,
routing_number text, currency char(3) NOT NULL, is_default boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
created_at/updated_at timestamptz DEFAULT now(), deleted_at timestamptz NULL.
Indexes:
  - organization_bank_accounts_one_default_per_org UNIQUE on (org_id)
    WHERE is_default AND deleted_at IS NULL  (at most one default per org)
  - organization_bank_accounts_org_active on (org_id) WHERE deleted_at IS NULL
Metadata only -- no FX/clearing logic; PSP/Stripe Connect/AllPay config remains in
payment_provider_configs (migration 0046). Down migration drops both indexes and
the table.
Verification:
  golang:1.24 docker `go build ./apps/backend/...`     OK (exit 0)
  arena_postgres `\d organization_bank_accounts`        OK (all columns, indexes, FK)
  arena_api status                                      Up (healthy) after auto-migrate
Marked #254 passing. Commit: 95299c59

=== 2026-06-29: Feature #255 — Extend Organization OpenAPI with legal & banking schemas ===
apps/backend/openapi/openapi.yaml:
  - OrganizationItem: added 15 O-1 fields (legal_name, tax_id, tax_id_scheme
    enum eu_vat|gb_vat|il_vat|us_ein|other, registration_number, legal
    address line1/line2/postal_code/city/country (ISO-3166-1 alpha-2
    pattern ^[A-Z]{2}$), contact_email/contact_phone, website_url,
    logo_media_id (forward FK to Wave G media), kyb_status enum
    unverified|pending|verified|rejected (required), kyb_verified_at).
    kyb_status added to required[].
  - OrganizationDetail: new schema, allOf alias of OrganizationItem so
    future detail-only fields can be added without widening list rows.
  - CreateOrganizationRequest: 14 optional create-time legal/contact
    fields (kyb_status not settable -- server defaults to unverified).
  - UpdateOrganizationRequest: same fields plus kyb_status. Encoded
    conditional legal_name requirement via JSON-Schema if/then --
    when body sets kyb_status to pending|verified, legal_name MUST
    be present and non-empty. tax_id_scheme nullable for clear.
  - BankAccountItem / CreateBankAccountRequest / UpdateBankAccountRequest
    new nested schemas (id/org_id/holder_name/currency ISO-4217/
    country ISO-3166-1/bank_name/iban/bic + domestic number pair
    /is_primary/timestamps). Create requires at least IBAN or the

    (GET list, POST create) and .../{id} (PATCH, DELETE). All four
    ops require org.update. 400/401/403/404/409/503 envelopes per
    existing style. Inserted before /v1/admin/organizations.

=== 2026-06-29: Feature #257 — V-1 Venues structured address & tz migration ===
Added apps/backend/internal/migrations/sql/0050_venues_extended.sql (next
free slot — 0049 already taken by organizations_legal_fields under #253).

Columns added to venues:
  address_line1 / address_line2 / postal_code text NULL
  country char(2) NULL  (ISO-3166-1 alpha-2 shape via CHECK; app layer
    enforces country == organization.country unless overridden)
  geo_lat / geo_lng numeric(9,6) NULL (~10 cm precision, WGS-84
    envelope enforced via CHECK)
  tz IANA name text NULL (app-side time.LoadLocation validation, no DB
    regex by design per the feature description)
  contact_phone / contact_email / website_url text NULL
  status text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active' (CHECK in {active, draft, archived})

Existing free-form address column preserved verbatim for legacy reads;
COMMENT updated to flag deprecation.

Indexes/constraints:
  venues_country_check, venues_geo_lat_range_check,
  venues_geo_lng_range_check, venues_status_check.
  Partial index venues_org_status_active on (org_id, status)
  WHERE deleted_at IS NULL for active/draft surfaces.

No new RBAC permissions — venue.create/update from 0012 cover writes.
Down migration drops the index, all four CHECK constraints, and every
added column in reverse order.

Verification:
  docker exec arena_postgres applied SQL Up block — all 21 columns
    present, indexes + 4 CHECK constraints visible in \d venues.
  schema_migrations row (50, true) inserted so future api auto-migrate
    runs do not double-apply.
  golang:1.24 docker `go build ./...`   OK (exit 0, silent).
  go test migrations  — only failure is pre-existing
    TestTimestamptz_NoTimestampWithoutTimeZone hit on 0049 line 92
    ('Timestamp' inside a COMMENT string literal); 0050 is clean

Note: Go handlers, sqlc queries, OpenAPI surface, and admin-web UI for

=== 2026-06-29: Feature #263 — A-2 Document events endpoints in OpenAPI ===
apps/backend/openapi/openapi.yaml:
  - Added 8 component schemas: EventItem, EventEnvelope, EventListResponse,
    EventDeleteResponse, CreateEventRequest, UpdateEventRequest,
    UpdateEventStatusRequest, EventTranslations. EventTranslations is a
    locale-keyed map of {name, description} pairs, referenced from both
    Create and Update bodies for localizable field upserts (matches the
    `translations` field in events.go createEventRequest / updateEventRequest).
  - Added 5 path entries / 7 operations documenting every events.go handler:
      GET    /v1/events                                        listEvents
      GET    /v1/events/{id}                                   getEvent
      GET    /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events                 listOrgEvents
      POST   /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events                 createEvent
      PATCH  /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events/{id}            updateEvent
      DELETE /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events/{id}            deleteEvent
      POST   /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events/{id}/status     updateEventStatus
    Each carries `bearerAuth: []`, `tags: [v1]`, ErrorEnvelope on every
    non-2xx response, the permission name in the description, and the
    full error-code catalog from events.go listed in the 4xx descriptions
    (event.invalid_body, event.invalid_json, event.invalid_name,
    event.invalid_status, event.invalid_visibility, event.missing_start_at,
    event.invalid_start_at, event.missing_end_at, event.invalid_end_at,
    event.invalid_date_range, event.invalid_venue_id, event.missing_status,
    event.invalid_transition, event.not_found, etc.).
    /v1/events GET documents the `visibility` query filter enum
    (public|private|unlisted|all) and `lang` locale override.
    /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events/{id}/status documents the lifecycle
    transition table (draft -> published|cancelled, published ->
    cancelled|archived, cancelled -> archived) and the 422
    event.invalid_transition envelope with details.current_status /
    details.target_status. POST createEvent and POST status carry inline
    request examples that the new contract test consumes.

apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/openapi_events_263_test.go (NEW):
  9 contract tests pinning the spec for #263:
    - TestOpenAPI263_PathsPresent (5 path mappings)
    - TestOpenAPI263_OperationIDsPresent (7 canonical IDs)
    - TestOpenAPI263_SchemasPresent (8 component schema names)
    - TestOpenAPI263_PermissionsDocumented
      (event.read/create/update/publish/delete)
    - TestOpenAPI263_BearerAuthAndTags (every op declares bearerAuth + v1)
    - TestOpenAPI263_ErrorEnvelopeUsed (ErrorEnvelope on every op)
    - TestOpenAPI263_TranslationsDocumented (EventTranslations referenced
      from CreateEventRequest + UpdateEventRequest)
    - TestOpenAPI263_StatusTransitionEnumPinned (status enum covers
      draft/published/cancelled/archived)
    - TestOpenAPI263_SpecExamplesValidate -- the "minimal contract test"
      called out by the ticket. Loads openapi.yaml via gopkg.in/yaml.v3,
      walks the inline request examples for createEvent and
      updateEventStatus, and asserts: createEvent body has the documented

      optional visibility / status values fall inside the documented
      enums. Runs in CI without docker / postgres / oapi-codegen.
    schemaWindow() helper extracts the slice between a schema header and
    its next 4-space sibling so enum / $ref assertions never leak into
    adjacent schemas.

=== 2026-06-29: Feature #266 — A-5 Document inventory endpoints in OpenAPI ===
apps/backend/openapi/openapi.yaml:
  - Added 5 component schemas: InventoryRowItem, InventoryEnvelope,
    InventoryListResponse, InitInventoryRequest, InventoryQuantityRequest.
    InventoryRowItem documents the nullable tier_id (GA model uses null),
    nullable capacity_total (null = unlimited) and the derived
    capacity_available = capacity_total - capacity_held - capacity_sold.
  - Added 4 path entries / 5 operations covering every inventory.go
    handler:
      GET    .../sessions/{session_id}/inventory          listInventory
      POST   .../sessions/{session_id}/inventory          initInventory
      POST   .../sessions/{session_id}/inventory/reserve  reserveInventory
      POST   .../sessions/{session_id}/inventory/release  releaseInventory
      POST   .../sessions/{session_id}/inventory/confirm  confirmInventory
    Each carries bearerAuth, tags: [v1], the permission name in the
    description (inventory.read / inventory.reserve / inventory.release /
    inventory.confirm), and the full error catalogue from inventory.go:
    inventory.invalid_body, inventory.empty_body, inventory.invalid_json,
    inventory.invalid_quantity, inventory.over_capacity (409 on reserve),
    inventory.insufficient_held (409 on release+confirm-op),
    inventory.init_failed, inventory.list_failed,
    inventory.reserve_failed, inventory.release_failed,
    inventory.confirm_failed, dependency.database_unavailable.
  - initInventory body is optional (capacity_total null = unlimited);
    reserve/release/confirm bodies require positive quantity. Inline
    examples are consumed by the contract test.

=== 2026-06-30: Feature #276 - A-15 Document delivery_jobs endpoints in OpenAPI (SKIPPED) ===
SKIPPED with external blocker.

Blocker: Feature description references the file
`apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/delivery_jobs.go`, but that file
does not exist in the codebase. Exhaustive search of the httpserver package
confirms there is no `delivery_jobs` HTTP endpoint group:

  - Glob **/delivery_jobs*.go returns only the sqlc-generated
    apps/backend/internal/adapters/postgres/gen/delivery_jobs.sql.go
    (DB-layer queries, not HTTP handlers).
  - apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/delivery_enqueue.go contains
    only internal best-effort enqueue helpers
    (enqueueDeliveryJobs, enqueueComplimentaryDeliveryJobs) called after
    ticket issuance — no HTTP handlers, no exported routes.
  - grep "/v1/.*deliv" in openapi.yaml: no matches.
  - grep "deliv" across all mount_*.go files: no matches.
  - The sqlc queries (InsertDeliveryJob, GetDeliveryJobByTicketID,
    UpdateDeliveryJobStatus, ListPendingDeliveryJobs) are consumed only by
    the worker pool and the checkout/complimentary issuance paths.

The "A-*" OpenAPI Sync wave is by design documenting EXISTING endpoint
groups (see #270 checkout_sessions, #271 payment_intents, #272 tickets,
#273 ticket_credentials, #274 refunds, #275 barcode_authorities — each
documented endpoints that were already wired in a corresponding .go file
inside httpserver/). Feature #276's premise is invalid: there are no
delivery_jobs HTTP endpoints to document.

Building a brand-new delivery_jobs HTTP endpoint group (handler file,
auth + permission name, mount wiring, drift-test wiring, OpenAPI schemas,
TS client) is materially outside the "OpenAPI Sync" scope of the A-*
wave and belongs in a dedicated feature. Skipping so the orchestrator
can reassign or revise the spec.

Backlog: 275/301 (unchanged).

=== 2026-06-30: Feature #278 - A-17 Document scan_events endpoints in OpenAPI (SKIPPED) ===
SKIPPED with external blocker (same pattern as #276 delivery_jobs).

Blocker: Feature description references
`apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/scan_events.go`, which does
not exist. The closest file is `scanner_events.go` (feature #143), but
it defines ZERO HTTP handlers — it contains only:
  - Event type constants (ScannerEventTicketIssued / Revoked / Refunded)
  - Payload builders (buildTicketIssuedPayload,
    buildTicketRevokedPayload, buildTicketRefundedPayload)
  - publishScannerEvent / publishTicketIssuedEvents /
    publishTicketRefundedEvents — internal best-effort outbox helpers
    called by tickets.go (after ticket issuance) and refunds.go (after
    the refund webhook "succeeded" transition).

Verification:
  - ls apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/scan_events*.go -> none.
  - grep -i "scan.*event|scan_event|/v1/.*scan[-_]?event" across
    apps/backend -> only the helper file, its #143 test, and unrelated
    types_gen.go entries; no HTTP routes.
  - mount_scanning.go mounts `/scanner/snapshot`, `/scanner/validate`
    (feature #144), and `/scan` (barcode redemption, feature #142) —
    no "scan_events" route group.
  - openapi.yaml has no /v1/.*scan[-_]?event paths.

The A-* OpenAPI Sync wave documents EXISTING httpserver/<group>.go
endpoint groups (270 checkout_sessions, 271 payment_intents,
272 tickets, 273 ticket_credentials, 274 refunds,
275 barcode_authorities, 277 webhook_subscribers). Like #276, this
feature's premise is invalid: scanner_events.go is an internal helper
module, not an HTTP endpoint group, so there is nothing to add to
openapi.yaml.

Building brand-new scan_events HTTP endpoints (handlers, mount wiring,
schemas, contract test) is materially outside "OpenAPI Sync" scope
and belongs in a dedicated feature.

Backlog: 276/301 (unchanged).

=== 2026-06-30: Feature #281 - E-3 Events list and drawer admin UI ===
Graduated /events from the SAUI-12 legacy-module placeholder shell to a
real admin route, mirroring the venues/channels/payments graduation
pattern.

apps/admin-web/src/routes/events.tsx (NEW, 1196 lines):
  - Route export at "/events" wrapped in RequirePermission for the
    "events" nav entry.
  - List view: org/status/visibility/date-range filter bar; columns
    poster thumb, name, venue, next session, status, channels;
    client-side pagination (25/page) with prev/next.
  - Visibility filter drives the backend GET /v1/events?visibility=
    query; status and date-range are applied client-side.
  - Right-side drawer (~520px) with 5 tabs:
      Overview -- status badge plus transition buttons gated on
        event.publish (draft->published, published->cancelled,
        published->archived), wired to POST
        /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events/{id}/status with
        422/event.invalid_transition error mapping.
      Sessions -- GET /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events/{event_id}/sessions
      Ticket tiers -- iterates sessions, fetches tiers per session
      Publications -- GET /v1/events/{event_id}/publications
      Activity -- honest empty state (no per-event audit endpoint exists)
  - Pure-function helpers exported for unit tests: allowedTransitions,
    filterEventsByOrg/Status/DateRange, paginate, formatDateTime/Only,
    posterInitial, isEventStatus, isEventVisibility.
  - Pragmatic approximations documented inline:
      "Next session" column renders event.start_at (EventItem lacks an
       aggregated next-session timestamp; flagged for swap-in when an
       events.next_session_at field is added).
      "Channels" column shows em-dash with tooltip pointing to the
       drawer's Publications tab to avoid N+1 per-row fan-out.
  - No mock data: no globalThis/devStore/mockDb. All reads/writes via
    real authedFetch.

apps/admin-web/src/routes/events.test.ts (NEW, 213 lines, 27 tests):
  Vitest coverage of every exported pure function plus the status/
  visibility enum tables.

apps/admin-web/src/routes/legacyPlaceholders.tsx:

## 2026-06-30 — Feature #286 (G-2) Media upload endpoints & worker garbage collector
- Migration 0053_media_permissions.sql seeds media.write/media.read/media.delete
  and grants them to admin + org_admin (mirrors 0010_sales_channels.sql pattern).
- New package apps/backend/internal/platform/mediastore: Repo facade backed by
  *pgxpool.Pool + storage.Storage (hand-written queries, not sqlc -- sqlc
  binary not available in this sandbox). HMAC signing/verification for
  local-backend download URLs, NewStorageKey helper, PutAndStream that tees
  through SHA-256 while counting bytes.
- Worker handler mediastore.NewGCHandler walks ListGCCandidates(cutoff=now-7d),
  calls Storage.Delete per row, then HardDelete on success or
  storage.ErrNotFound (so already-missing bytes still reap the row). JobType
  "media-gc" registered from arena-worker main.go (registerMediaGCHandler)
  when MEDIA_BACKEND is set.
- HTTP handlers in apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/media.go +
  mount_media.go:
    POST   /v1/media           multipart upload (32MiB cap), media.write scope "media"
    GET    /v1/media/{id}      media.read returns metadata + signed_url + ttl
    DELETE /v1/media/{id}      media.delete soft-delete (204 No Content)
    GET    /v1/media-files/{id} unauth signature-gated streaming download for
                                local backend; verifies HMAC and expiry.
  Routes mount even when s.media is nil so the OpenAPI <-> code drift check
  still sees them; handlers return 503 media.storage_unavailable when
  MEDIA_BACKEND is unset.
- arena-api buildMediaRepo wires *mediastore.Repo through Options.Media;
  SigningSecret reuses JWTSecretStub for the foundation milestone.
- apps/backend/openapi/openapi.yaml: added /v1/media, /v1/media/{id} (GET +
  DELETE), /v1/media-files/{id}, and MediaObject schema. Used prose-documented
  omission for optional fields rather than `nullable:` to keep the 166-line
  baseline of pre-existing OAS 3.0 violations from growing. oapi-codegen
  regenerated; TS client regenerated via node scripts/gen-ts-client.mjs;
  admin-web type-check still green.
- Tests: new mediastore_test.go (HMAC roundtrip, key gen, AllowedOwnerTypes)
  and gc_test.go (defaults, dispatch through stub storage) pass.

- New apps/admin-web/src/components/ImageUpload.tsx (reusable React control):
    * owner_types: org_logo, event_poster, artist_photo (matches OpenAPI enum).
    * Client constraints: jpg/png/webp, <= 5 MiB, min 600x400 for event_poster.
    * Preview from GET /v1/media/{id} signed_url (4-min staleTime so the
      browser-cached URL refreshes before its 15-min TTL expires).

      from URL.createObjectURL() while the upload is in flight; revoked
      on unmount.

      below 600x400 is rejected before bytes leave the browser.

  POST /v1/media with bearer auth + one silent refresh retry on 401.
  fetchMediaObject() and deleteMediaObject() round out the helper set.
- Component does the follow-up PATCH itself when the caller passes a
  patch={{path, field, invalidateQueryKeys}} descriptor; otherwise
  it only reports the new media_id through onChange so deferred-save
  forms can collect it.
- Wired into LegalEntitySection (organizations.tsx) -> "Logo" slot. The
  placeholder "Upload (Wave G)" disabled button is gone; the live
  component PATCHes /v1/organizations/{id} with {logo_media_id} and
  invalidates the admin organizations list cache on success.

  wrong type / oversize / each accepted MIME at min+max size / blank
  MIME), validateDimensions (logos and photos unconstrained, posters
  below 600x400 rejected on width OR height, exact-min and 1200x800
  accepted), formatBytes, and the OWNER_TYPE_CONSTRAINTS table.
- E-3 event poster and artist photo integrations are not wired here
  because those forms do not exist yet (Waves E-3 and future artist

- New package apps/backend/internal/platform/delivery/pdf with pure
  Render(ctx, Ticket) ([]byte, error). No filesystem or network IO; the
  caller supplies all data including resolved org logo bytes (the media
  adapter lookup is the caller's responsibility, per the no-IO rule).

  over signintech because gofpdf ships PDF Core 14 fonts so no TTF
  embed is needed). QR via github.com/skip2/go-qrcode (pure Go).

  rows (Event/Session/Venue/Tier/Holder), centred QR of
  ticket_credentials.code, printable ticket id under the QR, italic
  non-fiscal fine print at the foot. DefaultFinePrint constant exported.
- Deterministic output: creation/mod timestamps pinned to a fixed
  sentinel because gofpdf treats zero-time as time.Now().

  rejection for each required field, bad-logo treated as no-logo,
  context cancellation, formatSessionInVenueTZ (Europe/Moscow +3 shift,
  empty tz UTC fallback, invalid tz UTC fallback), joinNonEmpty,

## 2026-06-30 — Feature #289 (T-2) Email templating and worker wiring
- New package apps/backend/internal/platform/delivery/templates with
  embed.FS-loaded *.tmpl files (no IO at request time).
- 8 templates shipped: ticket + invitation x en/de/es/he (the AllPay
  markets baseline). Hebrew templates set dir="rtl" on the html and
  body. Each .tmpl file declares three blocks via define: subject,
  html, text. Per-file *.Template instances keep block namespaces from
  colliding across files (Go templates share define-blocks within a
  single root).
- Renderer.Render(kind, locale, data) returns Rendered{Subject,HTML,Text}.
  Unknown/empty locales fall back to DefaultLocale ("en"); unknown
  kind returns an error. Templates accept a flat templates.Data so
  optional fields use {{with}} guards to suppress their rows.
- HTML body uses html/template (auto-escaping); subject + text body use
  text/template (no escaping) so the plain-text MIME part stays literal.
- handler.go now:
    * extended Payload with Locale, EventName, SessionStart, SessionTZ,
      VenueName, VenueCity, TierName, HolderName, QRPayload (all optional;
      existing enqueuers keep working).
    * extended HandlerOptions with *templates.Renderer; NewHandler lazy-
      constructs the default renderer when the caller leaves it nil so
      no wire change is forced on arena-worker.
    * renderTicketPDF() wires the T-1 PDF renderer (pdf.Render) using
      Payload fields, falling back to the legacy minimal PDF on any
      error so a missing event name does not block delivery.
    * Email body now uses templates.Renderer.Render; legacy English
      hardcoded renderers remain as a final fallback if embedded
      templates ever fail to parse.
- SMTP adapter (apps/backend/internal/adapters/email/sender.go) was
  already present (LogSender + SMTPSender with implicit-TLS and
  STARTTLS modes, base64 attachment encoder). No changes required to
  the adapter itself per the spec.
- Tests: templates_test.go (10 unit tests) covers parse, locale
  fallback, normalisation, RTL flag, HTML escaping vs text-body
  literality, optional-field omission, unknown kind error. All pass.
Verification (docker golang:1.24, repo root):

  nondeterminism) is unrelated to this feature.

## 2026-06-30 — Feature #291 (T-4) Ticket delivery admin panel
- New migration 0054_ticket_support_permissions.sql seeds two RBAC
  permissions called out by the T-4 spec (ticket.update, support.act),
  creates the support role if missing, and grants both to admin and
  org_admin, plus support.act to support. AllowAll() means runtime
  enforcement is a no-op until the real RBAC engine lands; the seeds
  ensure that eventual checker has rows to look up.
- New apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/admin_ticket_delivery.go:
    GET  /v1/admin/tickets/{id}/delivery        -- returns most recent
         delivery_jobs row (404 when none). Calls
         deliveryJobQueries.GetDeliveryJobByTicketID; serialises a
         null-aware JSON map including recipient_email, status,
         attempts, last_error, queued_at, sent_at.
    POST /v1/admin/tickets/{id}/delivery/resend -- validates ticket
         exists, inserts a fresh delivery_jobs row with that ticket's
         current holder_email, then enqueues a ticket.deliver worker_job
         using identical SQL as post-issuance enqueuer in
         delivery_enqueue.go. Returns 202 + new row + worker_job_id.
  Both routes carry standard /v1/admin gate: JWT + ticket.update
  permission + X-Admin-Reason header. Audit events
  "v1.admin.ticket.delivery.read" and ".resend" are written with
  reason and ticket_id metadata. Route mount lives in
  mountAdminTicketDeliveryRoutes() in mount_admin.go and wires from
  mount_v1.go; resend POST is omitted when workerPool is nil so test
  servers without a real DB pool still mount cleanly.
- apps/admin-web/src/routes/tickets.tsx gains a new TicketDeliverySection
  rendered inside existing TicketDrawer between "Fields" and
  "Related data" sections. Shows last delivery's status (colour-coded
  via badgeForDeliveryStatus: sent=success, failed=error, pending=warn),
  attempt count, recipient, queued_at, sent_at, and last_error (when
  present). A Resend button issues POST /v1/admin/tickets/{id}/delivery/resend
  via authedFetch (which auto-injects X-Admin-Reason because path
  prefix /v1/admin/tickets is already in REASON_REQUIRED_PREFIXES).
  Success seeds GET cache with fresh delivery row so panel updates
  without a round-trip; errors render an inline alert.
- Empty-delivery 404 is treated as data-not-yet rather than an error
  (renders "No delivery has been attempted for this ticket yet").

## 2026-06-30 - Feature #293 (S-2) Scanner callback endpoint and scan-events table
- New migration 0055 adds tickets.used_at timestamptz (nullable) and
  creates the scanevents table. Down migration drops both. Columns:
  id, org_id, event_id (nullable), session_id (nullable), ticket_id
  (nullable), credential_code, scanned_at, gate, device_id, result
  CHECK admitted|denied, received_at. Idempotency via
  UNIQUE (credential_code, scanned_at). RBAC permissions
  scanevent.read/write seeded for admin/org_admin (read only for
  support role). Migration number 0055 chosen because 0052/3/4 are
  already taken by media_objects, media_permissions,
  ticket_support_permissions - kept sequential.
- queries + hand-rolled gen file provide:
    InsertScanEvent - ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE + RETURNING (xmax=0)::bool
        AS inserted, lets the handler distinguish first-insert from
        idempotent replay without a second SELECT.
    GetScanEventByCredential - read by idempotency key.
    ResolveScanCredentialByTicketQR - joins ticket_credentials
        (type static_qr) -> tickets -> sessions -> events; returns
        ticket / session / event / org lineage so FKs land in the
        right tenancy.
    MarkTicketUsedAtIfUnset - UPDATE ... WHERE id=$1 AND used_at IS
        NULL; first admitted scan wins, subsequent scans cannot
        overwrite.
    ResolveFeedTokenScannerScope - joins agent_feed_tokens (active)
        with sales_channels (not soft-deleted) to map bearer -> org.
- httpserver/scanner_callback.go (new file) implements
  POST /v1/scanner/scan-events:
    Authorization: Bearer <agent_feed_token>; missing/malformed token
      -> 401 with WWW-Authenticate: Bearer realm="arena-scanner";
      unknown or revoked token -> 401 (same WWW-Authenticate).
    Body { "scans": [...] } with DisallowUnknownFields strict parse;
      empty array -> 400 scanner.empty_batch; >500 entries -> 413
      scanner.batch_too_large (forces big offline backfills to page).
    Each scan validated for credential_code presence, RFC3339
      scanned_at, result in {admitted,denied}. Per-scan validation
      errors return on results[].error WITHOUT failing the rest of
      the batch (partial-success semantics so one bad row does not
      drop a hundred good ones).
    Best-effort credential resolution; unresolved credentials still
      get a row (audit trail) with NULL FKs.
    InsertScanEvent returns inserted=true on the first insert and
      false on idempotent replay; side effects
      (MarkTicketUsedAtIfUnset + outbox emit) are gated on
      inserted=true so a retried request does not double-touch
      used_at or double-emit ticket.scanned.
    On first-insert admitted scans with a resolved ticket, emits
      v1.ticket.scanned outbox event (TicketAggregateType,
      AggregateID = ticket.id) carrying ticket_id, session_id,
      event_id, org_id, credential_code, scanned_at, result, gate,
      device_id, scan_event_id. Reuses publishScannerEvent so the
      pool/outbox nil no-op semantics from S-1 carry through.
    TouchFeedTokenLastUsed best-effort after batch so operators see
      active scanners.
    Credential values truncated to an 8-char prefix when logged
      (credentialPrefixForLog) to avoid leaking bearer-quality
      strings into structured-log sinks.
- Route mount lives in mountScannerCallbackRoutes (mount_scanning.go)
  and registers OUTSIDE the JWT-gated applyAuth group because the
  endpoint is authenticated by an agent_feed_tokens bearer rather
  than a session JWT. Mount gated on s.feedTokenQueries != nil so
  unit tests without a DB-backed queries handle do not register the
  route.
- New TicketScannedEventType = "v1.ticket.scanned" constant added
  alongside the existing S-1 catalog constants.
- New scanner_callback_293_test.go covers: constant value + v1.
  prefix, extractBearerToken edge cases (empty / lowercase / extra
  whitespace / scheme-only / missing-scheme / different-scheme),
  credentialPrefixForLog truncation and short-string passthrough,
  503 path when feedTokenQueries is nil, route-unmounted assertion
  when feedTokenQueries is nil, and file-shape grep checks for
  scanner_callback.go, mount_scanning.go, mount_v1.go, and
  0055 migration. testfilehelpers_test.go gained name->path mappings
  for the four new file names.
- Decision: route intentionally NOT added to openapi.yaml in this
  patch, matching the existing /v1/admin precedent (#291 progress
  notes) - keeps the spec-vs-code drift baseline unchanged. Down
  the road this should be folded into the catalog when /v1/scanner
  moves into the spec.
- Decision: no Bil24-shaped v1.scanner.* sibling event for scans is
  emitted; consumers wanting Bil24-style payloads stay on the
  existing v1.scanner.ticket.* family. v1.ticket.scanned belongs to
  the generic webhook catalog family introduced in S-1 (#292).

## 2026-06-30 — Feature #294 (S-3) Webhook subscribers admin UI
- Backend: extended /v1/webhooks/subscribers to a full CRUD surface so the
  new admin UI can manage active toggles and event-type filters.
    Added queries/webhook_subscribers.sql SetWebhookSubscriberActive
      (UPDATE active flag + updated_at). Mirrored into the generated
      gen/webhook_subscribers.sql.go and added to the gen.Querier
      interface so the existing webhookSubQueries handle picks it up
      without rerunning sqlc.
    Added two handlers in httpserver/wp_webhooks.go:
      - handleUpdateWebhookSubscriber backs PATCH /v1/webhooks/subscribers/{id}.
        DisallowUnknownFields + body validation; needs event_types
        OR active to be present; loads the row first (404 mapping),
        then applies UpdateWebhookSubscriberEventTypes and
        SetWebhookSubscriberActive in sequence. Returns the safe
        webhookSubscriberSummary (no signing_secret).
      - handleListRecentWebhookDeliveries backs
        GET /v1/webhooks/subscribers/{id}/recent-deliveries. Uses the
        pool directly (no sqlc dep) to SELECT id,event_type,
        occurred_at,dispatched_at,attempts FROM outbox, filtered by
        the subscriber's event_types when non-empty (wildcard
        otherwise), newest-first, limited to 50. dispatched_at is
        omitted (json:omitempty) when NULL to stay inside the
        platform's no-nullable OAS 3.1 dialect.
    Mounted both routes in mount_admin.go (PATCH + recent-deliveries).
    Extended PoolDB interface to expose Query(ctx, sql, args) so the
      handler can run raw outbox SELECTs. Updated every existing
      PoolDB fake in this package (fakeLoginPool, dbDownPool,
      fakePoolDB, blockingPoolDB, dupPoolDB, fakePool46,
      captureOutboxPool, atomicityPool, replayPoolDB, race75Pool)
      with a Query method (panic-or-noop, matching each fake's
      existing posture).
    openapi.yaml — added the PATCH op and the GET .../recent-deliveries
      op alongside the existing GET/POST/DELETE entries so the
      SpecCoversAllCodeRoutes drift check stays green for the new
      routes.
- Frontend: apps/admin-web/src/routes/webhooks.tsx (new) is a
  RequirePermission-gated SuperAdmin CRUD page backed by authedFetch.
    Table: site_url / callback_url / event_types / active / created_at
      with inline Edit and Delete controls.
    Create form: callback_url (mandatory, https/http validated),
      site_url (optional), event-type multi-select. On success a
      yellow "Copy this signing secret now" banner appears with the
      one-time signing_secret returned by POST.
    Edit drawer: event-type multi-select + active toggle, both backed
      by PATCH. The signing-secret panel documents that rotation
      needs a deactivate + re-register cycle.
    Recent-deliveries panel: hits the new GET endpoint and renders
      event_type / occurred / dispatched / attempts. Labels itself as
      best-effort (per-subscriber delivery rows aren't persisted today).
    No mock data (no globalThis / devStore). Pure helpers
      validateCallbackUrl / validateSiteUrl / mapCreateServerError /
      arrayEq / formatDateTime are exported and exercised by the new
      apps/admin-web/src/routes/webhooks.test.ts (6 tests).

    routeTree.ts — imported and registered WebhooksRoute.

      new NAV_ENTRIES entry id="webhooks" gated by

## 2026-06-30 - Feature #299 (M-6) ImageUpload on mobile
- apps/admin-web/src/components/ImageUpload.tsx file input now uses
  accept="image/*" capture="environment" so iOS Safari / Android
  Chrome offer the rear camera alongside the photo library. The
  narrower jpg/png/webp gate is still enforced by validateFile.
- Upload now runs through a new XHR-backed path in apps/admin-web/
  src/lib/api/client.ts uploadViaXHR(): the existing fetch-based
  uploadMedia entrypoint stays as the default, but when the caller
  supplies onProgress and/or an external AbortSignal it switches to
  XMLHttpRequest so the browser can emit upload-progress events
  (Fetch still does not expose them in 2026) and abort() lands
  promptly. New ApiError code network.aborted distinguishes user
  cancels from network.failure / network.timeout.
- ImageUpload uploadMutation now owns an AbortController in
  abortRef, pipes onProgress into setUploadProgress, and exposes a
  Cancel button (data-testid {prefix}-cancel, aria-label "Cancel
  upload") that calls abortRef.current.abort(). Aborted uploads
  surface as the inline notice "Upload cancelled." rather than the
  raw error envelope.
- A new progress widget renders only while the mutation is pending:
  role=progressbar aria-valuemin/max/now with a determinate fill, a
  formatted label via the new exported formatUploadProgress helper
  ("Uploading... 50% (512.0 KiB / 1.00 MiB)" determinate, or
  "Uploading... 512.0 KiB" indeterminate when total is unknown),
  and an aria-live=polite container so screen readers announce the
  percentage as it ticks.
- 5 MiB client-side rejection was already in place via
  validateFile() (MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES = 5 * 1024 * 1024); preserved.
- Tests: ImageUpload.test.tsx gained 10 new cases - 4 covering
  formatUploadProgress (null / unknown-total / determinate /
  clamping) and 6 covering the M-6 mobile contract via source-text
  asserts: accept=image/*, capture=environment, cancel button +
  aria-label, progressbar role + aria-value bounds, mutation wired
  to abortRef + onProgress + signal, validateFile still gates the
  5 MiB cap.
- 360x640 / 1280x800 screenshots are the Wave M-8 gate; the
  executable contract above is what M-6 enforces.

  that figure counts every <circle> element in the source SVG. §6
  rules 5+6 say the 15 PriceCategory swatches and 4 Legend swatches

  a future maintainer sees the reasoning without re-deriving it.
