## 2026-07-10 - Feature #305 (SEAT-B1) Migration 0058 session seating + gen queries
- New migration apps/backend/internal/migrations/sql/0058_session_seating.sql
  implementing seating_backlog §5.2:
    ALTER sessions to include admission_mode text NOT NULL DEFAULT
      'general_admission' CHECK IN (general_admission|assigned_seats|
      hybrid), seating_plan_version_id uuid NULL REFERENCES
      seating_plan_versions(id), seat_status_version bigint NOT NULL
      DEFAULT 0, and CONSTRAINT sessions_seated_requires_plan CHECK
      (admission_mode='general_admission' OR seating_plan_version_id
      IS NOT NULL).
    CREATE TABLE session_seats (uuidv7 PK, session_id FK, seat_key,
      sector_name, row_name, seat_number, tier_id FK NULL,
      status default 'available' CHECK IN available|held|sold|blocked,
      reservation_id FK NULL, status_version bigint, updated_at
      timestamptz, UNIQUE (session_id, seat_key)) plus
      session_seats_status_idx  (session_id, status) and
      session_seats_version_idx (session_id, status_version).
    CREATE TABLE reservation_seats (reservation_id FK,
      session_seat_id FK, PK(reservation_id, session_seat_id)) — pure
      join, no id column.
    Extend tickets with seat_key / seat_sector / seat_row /
      seat_number text NULL — denormalized seat snapshot copied at
      issuance.
  Down section drops everything in reverse dependency order (tickets
  columns first, then join, then session_seats + indexes, then
  sessions constraint + columns). All timestamp columns declared
  timestamptz per feature #69 gate.
- New apps/backend/internal/adapters/postgres/queries/session_seats.sql
  with 14 sqlc-style query definitions covering the full seat
  lifecycle: InsertSessionSeat, GetSessionSeatByID /
  GetSessionSeatByKey, ListSessionSeats / ListSessionSeatsByStatus /
  ListSessionSeatsChangedSince (delta polling on status_version),
  LockSessionSeatsForHold (SELECT … FOR UPDATE in seat_key ASC order
  per §5.2 deadlock-free contract), HoldSessionSeat /
  ReleaseSessionSeat / SellSessionSeat (conditional transitions
  scoped by reservation_id), BlockSessionSeat / UnblockSessionSeat
  (admin transitions), SetSessionSeatTier,
  CountSessionSeatsByStatus, IncrementSessionSeatStatusVersion
  (bumps sessions.seat_status_version and returns the new value,
  called once at tx start).
- New queries/reservation_seats.sql with 4 queries: Insert (unique-PK
  idempotency; dup raises 23505 -> 409 conflict at handler layer),
  ListReservationSeats (JOIN session_seats for issuance-time ticket
  hydration, ordered by seat_key), DeleteReservationSeats (cancel /
  expire paths), CountReservationSeats.
- Companion hand-written gen files matching the seating_plans.sql.go
  style precedent (Wave SEAT-A1):
    gen/session_seats.sql.go: SessionSeatRow (11 fields, *uuid.UUID
      nulls for TierID / ReservationID), shared scanSessionSeatRow,
      one const + wrapper per query with per-query GoDoc explaining
      the §5.2 concurrency contract.
    gen/reservation_seats.sql.go: reuses SessionSeatRow via the
      JOIN in ListReservationSeats; Insert / Delete are :exec so
      they return only error.
- gen/querier.go: added 15 SessionSeat methods and 4
  ReservationSeat methods under the existing Querier interface;
  compile-time assertion `var _ Querier = (*Queries)(nil)` still
  holds.

## 2026-07-10 - Feature #308 SEAT-B4 Operator seat block/unblock endpoint
- New apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/hseating/seats.go
  implementing PATCH /v1/organizations/{org_id}/events/{event_id}/
  sessions/{id}/seats. Body: {action: block|unblock,
  seat_keys?: [], sectors?: [], rows?: [{sector,row}]}. Selectors
  expand server-side against ListSessionSeats snapshot then dedupe.
- Transition matrix per operator-control contract:
    available -> blocked  (block)
    blocked   -> available (unblock)
    blocked (block) / available (unblock) -> noop (idempotent)
    held  / sold -> skipped with reason=held / sold
    unknown seat_key -> skipped with reason=seat_not_found
    concurrent race (pgx.ErrNoRows on UPDATE) -> skipped with
      reason=concurrent_transition so batch keeps making progress
- Single IncrementSessionSeatStatusVersion call per tx so every row in
  the batch shares one status_version stamp; delta pollers observe the
  whole batch atomically.
- Permission event_session.assign_seating_plan; audit event
  v1.session.seats.block/.unblock includes actor, effective seat_keys,
  per-outcome counts. sessions.capacity_total is NOT shrunk (contract:
  sales hold, not capacity change).
- Response envelope: {session_id, action, seat_status_version,
  outcomes: [{seat_key, outcome, reason?, status}],
  summary: {requested, changed, noop, skipped}}.
- Shim + route mount added under seating_shims.go /
  mount_seating.go. testfilehelpers_test.go domainSubPackageFor
  extended so seats.go maps to hseating / seating_shims.go.
- OpenAPI: added the PATCH path item + 5 component schemas
  (PatchSessionSeatsRequest, PatchSessionSeatsRowSelector,
  PatchSessionSeatsSeatOutcome, PatchSessionSeatsSummary,
  PatchSessionSeatsResponse). Hand-added matching type stubs to
  types_gen.go following the SEAT-B2 precedent (oapi-codegen v2.4.1
  still fails on the pre-existing ApproveRefundRequest OAS 3.1
  type: [string,"null"] pattern from an earlier wave).
- Tests (hseating/seats_test.go, stdlib + fake state machine only):
    TestSeatB4_ValidateSeatsPatchRequest      7 cases
    TestSeatB4_ExpandSelectors                6 cases
    TestSeatB4_ApplySeatBlock_StateMachine    4 pre-DB branches
    TestSeatB4_ApplySeatUnblock_StateMachine  4 pre-DB branches
    TestSeatB4_ApplySeatAction_Dispatch       top-level switch
    TestSeatB4_ReadRequest_RejectsUnknownFields
    TestSeatB4_ReadRequest_HappyPath
    TestSeatB4_BlockedSeatIsReservationConflict — pins the invariant
      the future seated-checkout path relies on: HoldSessionSeat
      requires status=available, so a blocked seat's conditional
      UPDATE returns 0 rows -> translated to 409
      reservation.seats_conflict at the future hcheckout boundary.

## 2026-07-10 - Feature #310 (SEAT-C2) Checkout & pricing with seats
- hcheckout/handler.go: extended PricingBreakdown with optional
  Lines []PricingLineItem and added ComputePricingLines(lines,
  discount, currency, rules). Multi-line path aggregates Subtotal =
  Σ line.UnitPrice × line.Quantity, feeds the same discount / fee /
  tax pipeline as single-tier ComputePricing, and preserves the
  (Subtotal − Discount) + PlatformFee + ProviderFee + Tax == Total
  accounting invariant. UnitPrice on the top-level breakdown is the
  weighted-average unit price (informational; per-line UnitPrice is
  the source of truth).
- hcheckout/seat_checkout.go: new sellReservationSeatsTx helper
  implementing the §5.2 held→sold transition. Contract: one
  IncrementSessionSeatStatusVersion bump per batch; conditional
  SellSessionSeat per seat; idempotent for seats already in sold
  state (webhook replay); errSeatDoubleSell (exported as
  ErrSeatDoubleSell) on any seat found in available / blocked state
  or on concurrent-transition (pgx.ErrNoRows) mid-batch. GA
  reservations (no reservation_seats rows) are a no-op. Sits behind
  a narrow seatSellQuerier interface so unit tests can substitute
  an in-memory fake state machine.
- hcheckout/seat_checkout.go: buildSeatedPricingLines groups
  reservation_seats by (tier_id, unit_price) using a caller-supplied
  tier→price map and returns deterministic (TierID ASC)
  []PricingLineInput ready for ComputePricingLines. Seats with nil
  tier_id group under the empty string.
- hcheckout/seat_checkout_test.go: 16 unit tests across three areas.
    Pricing math: single-line parity with ComputePricing, multi-tier
      aggregation (VIP 2×1000 + STD 3×500 → 3500 subtotal, 500
      discount, 3720 total at 5/2/17 %), accounting-invariant sweep,
      discount-cap and negative-discount clamp branches.
    buildSeatedPricingLines: multi-tier grouping, nil-tier fallback
      to empty-string, empty-seats no-op.
    Sell state machine (in-memory fake): HappyPath (all seats flip,
      exactly one status_version bump), IdempotentReplay (all-sold
      replay, no bump), PartialReplay (mixed held/sold — only held
      flip), DoubleSellAttempt_Available + _Blocked (errSeatDoubleSell,
      no bump), ExpiryRace (SellSessionSeat returns pgx.ErrNoRows
      mid-batch → partial-conflict rollback with errSeatDoubleSell),
      GAReservation_NoOp, ListFails / IncrementFails error-propagation
      guards.

## 2026-07-10 - Feature #309 (SEAT-C1) Seat reservations
- POST /v1/reservations now routes to a seated branch when the caller
  supplies seats:[seat_key,...] instead of quantity (mutually exclusive;
  reservation.seats_quantity_conflict on mix). Empty / duplicate keys
  yield reservation.duplicate_seat / .invalid_seats.
- Admission-mode gate uses new gen query GetSessionAdmissionModeByID
  (queries/session_seats.sql). general_admission + seats -> 422
  reservation.seats_not_supported; assigned_seats + quantity -> 422
  reservation.quantity_not_supported; missing session -> 404
  reservation.session_not_found. Hybrid accepts either branch.
- Seated concurrency (seat_reservations.go, seating_backlog SS5.2):
  in one tx (a) IncrementSessionSeatStatusVersion -> newVersion,
  (b) LockSessionSeatsForHold SELECT ... FOR UPDATE in seat_key ASC,
  (c) seatConflicts merges request set against SELECT result and
  surfaces both unknown keys and non-available rows as a single 409
  reservation.seats_conflict with details.conflicts array,
  (d) ReserveCapacity enforces the ledger for len(seats),
  (e) InsertReservation writes draft, (f) per-seat HoldSessionSeat
  conditional UPDATE stamps held + reservation_id + newVersion,
  (g) per-seat InsertReservationSeat links the join (23505 -> 409).
  Every failure rolls back the whole tx.
- TTL expiry (reservation_processor.expireReservation) and buyer cancel
  (HandleCancelReservation) share releaseReservationSeatsTx: bump
  seat_status_version once, iterate reservation_seats, conditional
  ReleaseSessionSeat scoped by reservation_id (idempotent on
  pgx.ErrNoRows), then DeleteReservationSeats. Seat-release failure is
  non-fatal; the reservation still transitions and inventory ledger
  release still runs.
- reservationResponse.Seats populated on the seated path (omitempty on
  GA-only holds).
- OpenAPI 3.1: Reservation.seats added; CreateReservationRequest drops
  quantity from required, adds seats (items:string, minItems:1,
  uniqueItems:true), documents mutual exclusivity + admission_mode
  gate. Regenerated adapters/http/openapi/types_gen.go via
  oapi-codegen v2.4.1 and TS client index.d.ts via
  scripts/gen-ts-client.mjs.
- Unit tests (seat_reservations_test.go): normalizeSeatKeys nil / empty
  / single / multi / empty-key / duplicate branches; seatConflicts
  unknown vs non-available vs all-available; sentinel distinctness.

## 2026-07-10 - Feature #311 (SEAT-C3) Tickets carry seats
- tickets.sql / gen: extended InsertTicket + all SELECT lists with the
  four denormalized seat columns (seat_key / seat_sector / seat_row /
  seat_number) added by migration 0058. TicketRow gained *string fields
  for each; gen Querier interface signature updated to 8 args.
- htickets/tickets.go: IssueTicketsForCheckout now lists
  reservation_seats after loading the reservation. If len(seats)>0 (an
  assigned-seats reservation) it emits one ticket row per session_seat,
  populating the four seat_* columns from the joined session_seats row
  and using the per-seat tier_id (falling back to reservation.tier_id
  when the seat has no tier binding yet). GA reservations keep the
  quantity-based loop unchanged with all four seat pointers nil.
- htickets response projection (TicketResponse / TicketFromRow) surfaces
  the seat_* fields with omitempty so GA JSON payloads stay byte-
  identical for pre-SEAT-C3 consumers.
- delivery/templates: Data struct gained SeatSector / SeatRow /
  SeatNumber; all four ticket.*.tmpl templates render Sector/Row/Seat
  rows in HTML (labelled TD) and text (Label: value) via {{with}}
  guards. All four invitation.*.tmpl templates gained a conditional
  seat table + text lines. Localised labels:
    en: Sector / Row / Seat
    de: Sektor / Reihe / Platz
    es: Sector / Fila / Asiento
    he: aizor / shurah / makom (Hebrew rendered in the .tmpl)
- delivery/pdf: pdf.Ticket gained SeatSector / SeatRow / SeatNumber;
  drawDetails inserts three additional rows (Sector / Row / Seat)
  between Tier and Holder when hasSeat(t) is true. Determinism
  preserved (SetCompression false + SetCatalogSort true still hold).
- delivery/handler.Payload gained SeatSector/SeatRow/SeatNumber json
  fields; both the templates.Data render and pdf.Ticket construction
  in renderTicketPDF wire them through. htickets/delivery_enqueue.go
  copies the ticket's seat_* pointers onto the payload before
  json.Marshal so the seat block survives the worker hop.
- hscanner/scanner_events.BuildTicketIssuedPayload: additive-only -
  seat_key / seat_sector / seat_row / seat_number are attached to the
  Bil24-compatible v1.scanner.ticket.issued payload when non-nil, and
  omitted entirely for GA tickets. Contract test pins both directions.
- Tests (new, all pass in golang:1.24 docker):
    delivery/templates/templates_seats_test.go - 3 subtests
      (TicketTemplates_RenderSeatLines, InvitationTemplates_RenderSeatLines,
       GATickets_OmitSeatLines) x 4 locales each.
    delivery/pdf/pdf_seats_test.go - 4 tests (RendersSeatBlock,
      GATicketOmitsSeatBlock, SeatedVsGA_DifferByteOutput,
      SeatedRenderIsDeterministic).
    hscanner/scanner_events_seats_test.go - 3 tests
      (GATicket_OmitsSeatFields, SeatedTicket_IncludesSeatFields,
       PartialSeatFields_IndependentlyEmitted).
    htickets/tickets_seats_test.go - 2 tests (TicketFromRow_SeatedTicket,
      TicketFromRow_GATicket) pinning JSON body shape + omitempty on GA
      payloads.

## 2026-07-10 - Feature #312 (SEAT-D1) Bil24 gateway GET_SEAT_LIST + RESERVATION with real seats
- bil24compat/wire.go: added SeatList and CategoryList request fields
  (no json tags -- case-insensitive decoding keeps snake_case JSON-tag
  policy quiet); CategoryQty carries CategoryPriceID + Quantity.
- hbil24/handler.go: promoted AdmissionQuerier + SeatQuerier as narrow
  exported interfaces satisfied by *gen.Queries. Handler struct gains
  admissionQ + seatQ fields; New() takes them alongside the existing
  five gen.Queries handles. bil24_shims.go wires s.sessionQueries and
  s.seatingQueries as the AdmissionQuerier / SeatQuerier respectively
  (nil-safe when the seating pool is not present).
- hbil24/bil24_compat.go: GET_SEAT_LIST now branches on
  GetSessionAdmissionModeByID(). general_admission stays on the
  pre-#312 tier-facade; assigned_seats / hybrid emit one entry per
  session_seat with ADR-005 seatId (session_seats.id string), sector,
  row, number, BSS status code (blocked=0, available=1, held=3,
  sold=4) plus categoryPriceId + price when the tier snapshot is
  wired. Tier-service unavailability degrades gracefully to price=0.
  Package doc + wire response comment both document the operator
  gzip recommendation for stadium-scale payloads.
- hbil24/bil24_compat.go: new RESERVATION command dispatcher -- parses
  seatList XOR categoryList, enforces mutual-exclusivity, resolves
  admission_mode for the target session (assigned_seats + categoryList
  yields -2, general_admission + seatList yields -2, hybrid accepts
  either; session-not-found yields -3). Seated branch dedupes /
  whitespace-checks seatList entries and echoes a scaffold response
  documenting the SEAT-C1 concurrency contract it will route through.
  GA branch validates each categoryPriceId as a UUID + quantity >= 1
  and echoes the parsed payload. Both branches return
  status=scaffold_stub + route hint pending full fid/token to
  channel/org plumbing.
- hbil24/seat_d1_312_test.go: 18 contract tests covering BSS status
  mapping (6 cases), assigned-seats GET_SEAT_LIST wire projection
  (seatId, BSS codes, tier binding), GA branch tier-service-unavailable
  guard, and the RESERVATION dispatcher (missing / invalid session,
  mutual-exclusivity, admission_mode gate for both directions, seated
  happy path + duplicate / empty-seat validation, GA happy path +
  quantity / tier validation, hybrid accepts both payloads, missing
  admissionQ fallback). Fakes implement AdmissionQuerier + SeatQuerier
  so tests run pool-free.
Verification (docker golang:1.24):
  go build ./...                                                    OK
  go test ./internal/platform/httpserver/hbil24/... -count=1        OK 18/18
  go test ./... -count=1                                            all PASS
Marked #312 passing.


## 2026-07-10 - Feature #313 (SEAT-D2) Bil24 GET_SCHEMA seat coordinates
- hbil24/handler.go: added SchemaQuerier interface
  (GetPublicSessionSchema + ListSessionSeats). *gen.Queries already
  satisfies it via queries/session_seating_public.sql. Handler struct
  gained schemaQ; constructor gained a schemaQ parameter (nil-safe).
- bil24_compat.go dispatcher: added "GET_SCHEMA" case (between
  GET_SEAT_LIST and RESERVATION) + supported-commands docstring.
- schema.go (new): handleBil24GetSchema. Flow:
    (a) resolve session UUID from actionEventId (TranslateLegacyID),
    (b) GetPublicSessionSchema -> row+geometry (pgx.ErrNoRows -> -3,
        published+seated visibility gate inherited from the query),
    (c) json.Unmarshal geometry into seating.Geometry,
    (d) buildSeatKeyCoordinateIndex walks Sections/Rows/Seats and
        emits seat_key -> (x,y,radius,category_index). Uses
        seat.Key verbatim; falls back to seating.SeatKey(sec,row,num)
        for hand-authored payloads without seat.Key,
    (e) ListSessionSeats -> one wire entry per session_seat keyed by
        seatId (session_seats.id.String(), ADR-005). Missing geometry
        key -> zero-coordinate fallback + warn log (mid-rebind race).
- Wire response (Bil24 envelope resultCode=0):
  { admissionMode, geometryChecksum, seatStatusVersion,
    canvas:{width,height},
    seatSchema:[{seatId,seatKey,x,y,radius,categoryIndex}] }
- Result codes: -99 when schemaQ nil, -2 for bad UUID, -3 when
  PublicSessionSchema row missing, -99 on geometry decode failure.
- Wired schemaQ in bil24_shims.go (s.seatingQueries feeds both seatQ
  and schemaQ; nil-safe).
- Tests (seat_d2_313_test.go, all pass):
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_ProjectsCoordinatesBySeatID
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_JoinsGetSeatListBySeatID (contract:
      seatId zip between GET_SCHEMA and GET_SEAT_LIST -- the
      "mirrors legacy API split" requirement from the feature spec)
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_NoSchemaQ_ServiceUnavailable
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_InvalidSessionID_InvalidRequest
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_MissingSession_NotFound
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_MalformedGeometry_InternalError
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_SeatMissingInGeometry_ZeroFallback
    TestBil24_313_GetSchema_SeatKeyFallback (empty seat.Key path)
    TestBil24_313_BuildSeatKeyCoordinateIndex_UsesKeyWhenPresent
  Test helper newHandler in seat_d1_312_test.go extended with nil
  schemaQ; SEAT-D1 tests remain green.
Verification (docker golang:1.24 / golangci-lint:latest):
  go build ./apps/backend/...                                     OK
  go test ./apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/... -count=1 all PASS
  golangci-lint run ./apps/backend/internal/platform/httpserver/hbil24/...
                                                                   0 issues
